These attacks can compromise payment channels and potentially steal funds from participants. Riard expressed concerns about the challenges this poses to the Bitcoin ecosystem and the need for potential changes at the base-layer, which would require the buy-in of the entire Bitcoin community. He emphasized the need for utmost transparency in making any such alterations to the Bitcoin network. While the Lightning Network has gained popularity since its inception in 2018, it still faces criticisms about complexity and user experience.
